3250<div>

3251<h1>

3252Ultimate Guide to 9 Best Wood Kitchen Cabinets</h1>

3253

3254

3255<h2>

3256<span style="color:#696969;">

3257<em>

3258Bring Nature Indoors with Stunning Wood Cabinetry</em>

3259</span>

3260</h2>

3261

3262</div>

3263</div>

3264</div>

3265</div>

3266<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cc--b-bf-aeeef">

3267<div>

3268<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3269<div>

3270<h6>

3271By Mikael Short</h6>

3272

3273

3274<h6>

3275March 3, 2022</h6>

3276

3277</div>

3278</div>

3279</div>

3280</div>

3281</div>

3282</div>

3283</div>

3284</div>

3285</div>

3286</div>

3287</div>

3288</div>

3289</div>

3290<div class="">

3291<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-cbcc-c--af-ddcedfa">

3292<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-cbcc-c--af-ddcedfa">

3293<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3294<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3295<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3296<div class="">

3297<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bcc-ea-f-f-babe">

3298<div class="merce-column-container">

3299<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ceb--d--ebfe">

3300<div>

3301<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3302<div>

3303<p>

3304Wood cabinets&mdash;whether a solid hardwood or a veneer&mdash;are a staple in any kitchen, thanks to their design versatility and overall strength and natural beauty. As cabinets are the foundational statement feature, they create both the functional and aesthetic backbone of your kitchen.</p>

3305

3306

3307<p>

3308<a href="https://vevano.com/page/wood-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

3309Wood kitchen cabinets</a>

3310 in particular are popular for both their appearance, durability, and functionality. They are so versatile they can be easily matched with other design elements in your kitchen.</p>

3311

3312</div>

3313</div>

3314</div>

3315</div>

3316<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cd-c-a-be-acceca">

3317<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf cd-c-a-be-acceca-singleImageAlignment">

3318<a href="https://vevano.com/page/interior-design-services/">

3319<img class="cd-c-a-be-acceca-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/qfuzDMpb6GxWCXhsafxsznj1r4p5nS2aPkGkVXlmbnw/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci9zaGFrZXItc3R5bGUtY2FiaW5ldHMvY2FiaW5ldC1hcnRpY2xlLWNhbGxvdXQtd2ViLmpwZw" alt="free cabinet design consultation for wood cabinets with vevano home design services" title="free cabinet design consultation for wood cabinets with vevano home design services"/>

3320</a>

3321</div>

3322</div>

3323<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fbba-fe--d-ecda">

3324<div>

3325<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3326<div>

3327<p>

3328Even if you can&rsquo;t afford solid wood cabinets, there are a variety of wood-looking alternatives that can be just as beautiful and, in some cases, more durable.</p>

3329

3330

3331<p>

3332There are four degrees types of wood cabinets to be aware of:</p>

3333

3334

3335<ul>

3336

3337 <li>

3338<strong>

3339Solid Hardwood</strong>

3340 - The classic, timeless, and unique wood cut and carved into cabinetry, highlighting the natural beauty and strength of wood pieces.</li>

3341

3342 <li>

3343<strong>

3344Engineered Wood</strong>

3345 - As an alternative to real wood, engineered wood creates a slab made of several layers of sliced wood, glued and pressed together with heat and thermofused melamine to create a board with a wood-grain texture surface.</li>

3346

3347 <li>

3348<strong>

3349Veneer</strong>

3350 - A thin piece of wood attached to a manufactured, composite interior piece, offering the look of wood cabinets.</li>

3351

3352 <li>

3353<strong>

3354Laminate</strong>

3355 - A composite plank topped with a laminate layer bearing the appearance of your choice.</li>

3356

3357</ul>

3358

3359

3360<p>

3361There are a variety of ways to achieve a wood-look with your kitchen cabinets, depending on your budget, style, and durability needs.</p>

3362

3363</div>

3364</div>

3365</div>

3366</div>

3367</div>

3368</div>

3369</div>

3370</div>

3371</div>

3372</div>

3373</div>

3374</div>

3375</div>

3376<div class="">

3377<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-becaf-f-fdb-cbe-dcbab">

3378<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-becaf-f-fdb-cbe-dcbab">

3379<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3380<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3381<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3382<div class="">

3383<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-fcd-f---dbccb">

3384<div class="merce-column-container">

3385<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ccbae-a-d-bc-eeecb">

3386<div>

3387<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3388<div>

3389<h2>

3390Types of Wood Cabinets</h2>

3391

3392</div>

3393</div>

3394</div>

3395</div>

3396<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-afef-ce--ac-cddcdf">

3397<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf afef-ce--ac-cddcdf-singleImageAlignment">

3398<img class="afef-ce--ac-cddcdf-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/-EndZAaItbGL4gOniVyoFg3D2PDh1KOQiRU4KAKWN3g/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci93b29kLWNhYmluZXQtdHlwZXMvd29vZC1jYWJpbmV0LXR5cGVzLXdlYi5qcGc" alt="types of wood cabinets: including alder, hickory, poplar, maple, oak, cherry, and walnut kitchen wood cabinets" title="types of wood cabinets: including alder, hickory, poplar, maple, oak, cherry, and walnut kitchen wood cabinets"/>

3399</div>

3400</div>

3401<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ddb-ec--cc-aabde">

3402<div>

3403<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3404<div>

3405<p>

3406Wood cabinets are available in many different colors, shades, and species (tree type), providing a wide range of wood-grain variations and characteristics. The grain is the texture, markings, and pattern on the wood.</p>

3407

3408

3409<p>

3410Note that the best woods are both sturdy and beautiful. The most durable woods for kitchen cabinets have higher densities to ensure long-lasting <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets/" target="_blank">

3411cabinets</a>

3412.</p>

3413

3414

3415<p>

3416Below are the different wood species you&rsquo;ll find in cabinetry, their defining characteristics, and what kitchen design and <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets/" target="_blank">

3417cabinet styles</a>

3418 they work well in. Note that you don&rsquo;t need solid hardwood cabinets to get the look of Maple, Cherry, Walnut, and other wood cabinet varieties. All wood cabinet pictures are from our popular and customizable <a href="https://vevano.com/product/50658-wf-pie-foxcroft-piedmont-10x10-kitchen-cabinets/" target="_blank">

3419Foxcroft 10x10 Kitchen Cabinet Collections</a>

3420.</p>

3421

3422</div>

3423</div>

3424</div>

3425</div>

3504<h3>

3505Maple Cabinets</h3>

3506

3507

3508<p>

3509Hard maple is fine grain, light color wood with minimal color variation, offering a fairly uniform appearance. It often features well with a clear or natural finish to enhance its lighter tones, though it is easy to paint or stain too.</p>

3510

3511

3512<p>

3513It is more expensive than oak, though it is less dense. Maple is very durable and withstands temperatures better than other hardwoods. Often used for semi-custom and <a href="https://vevano.com/page/custom-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

3514custom cabinets</a>

3515.</p>

3516

3517

3518<p>

3519<em>

3520Popular for light contemporary or farmhouse styles.</em>

3521</p>

3522

3562<h3>

3563Cherry Cabinets</h3>

3564

3565

3566<p>

3567Cherry is a hardy and strong wood that features a smooth, fine-grain pattern that is beautiful whether it&rsquo;s natural or stained. It&rsquo;s considered a high-end wood type.</p>

3568

3569

3570<p>

3571The color varies between red to reddish brown in warm tones. Cherry is unique in that it darkens with age and sun exposure. It is often stained for uniform appearance throughout.</p>

3572

3573

3574<p>

3575<em>

3576Popular in contemporary or traditional styles.</em>

3577</p>

3578

3618<h3>

3619Walnut Cabinets</h3>

3620

3621

3622<p>

3623Walnut features a smooth uniform grain, like swirls, from deep chocolate brown to light reddish gray. It&rsquo;s also easy to carve. Walnut tends to mellow, or lighten, with age, making it a premium wood choice for kitchen cabinets.</p>

3624

3625

3626<p>

3627<em>

3628Popular for traditional, classic, and transitional styles.</em>

3629</p>

3670<h3>

3671Hickory Cabinets</h3>

3672

3673

3674<p>

3675Very strong and bearing a similar grain to oak, Hickory carries a wide variation in tone and color. It features tones from a pale cream, to a warm reddish light brown, or even black. Hickory is highlighted best with clear or natural finish.</p>

3676

3677

3678<p>

3679<em>

3680Popular with rustic or farmhouse styles.</em>

3681</p>

3757<h3>

3758Red Oak Cabinets</h3>

3759

3760

3761<p>

3762Red oak features distinct curved and straight grain patterns. Very hardy, strong, durable, and moderately priced, making it a favorite for kitchen cabinets. Red oak works with a variety of styles and finishes. If it&rsquo;s painted, it may still reveal its grain beneath.</p>

3763

3764

3765<p>

3766<em>

3767Popular in traditional styles.</em>

3768</p>

3809<h3>

3810White Oak Cabinets</h3>

3811

3812

3813<p>

3814Compared to red oak, white oak cabinets feature a subtler grain with more of a golden tone. A bit stronger than and just as durable as red oak, lending to a little bit of a higher price tag. White oak is used more in custom cabinetry. It&rsquo;s not recommended to stain white oak as it could put too much contrast into the grain.</p>

3815

3816

3817<p>

3818<em>

3819Popular in farmhouse, rustic, and period styles.</em>

3820</p>

3861<h3>

3862Alder Cabinets</h3>

3863

3864

3865<p>

3866Alder wood features a straight, fine-textured grain, much like cherry and maple. It&rsquo;s a lightweight hardwood (referred to as semi-hardwood) that&rsquo;s fairly uniform in color, light brown with reddish undertones. It&rsquo;s considered eco-friendly and easy to work with. You can use its natural grain and color or even stain it.</p>

3867

3868

3869<p>

3870<em>

3871Popular for rustic modern and contemporary styles.</em>

3872</p>

3913<h3>

3914Birch Cabinets</h3>

3915

3916

3917<p>

3918Birch is a durable and versatile fine-grain wood and is commonly used for moderately affordable cabinets. Its grain runs slightly darker than maple. Even though it&rsquo;s prone to inconsistent coloring, birch wood also takes finishes well, so it can be stained to resemble more luxury wood, like cherry or maple. Birch tends to be more expensive than engineered wood.</p>

3919

3920

3921<p>

3922<em>

3923Birch can work in a variety of styles due to its versatility.</em>

3924</p>

4000<h3>

4001Poplar Cabinets</h3>

4002

4003

4004<p>

4005Poplar wood is one of the strongest softwoods, and one of a couple soft woods available in cabinetry. It carries a uniform, light wood appearance, and it&rsquo;s being growing in popularity due to how affordable it is.</p>

4006

4007

4008<p>

4009It&rsquo;s lightweight yet strong, versatile, and easy to paint (though it may require more paint than you think when repainting). With how soft it is, it is prone to denting and scratches.</p>

4010

4011

4012<p>

4013<em>

4014Popular with farmhouse, rustic, contemporary, and modern styles.</em>

4015</p>

4043<h2>

4044Cost of Wood Cabinets</h2>

4045

4046

4047<p>

4048The <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-much-do-kitchen-cabinets-cost/" target="_blank">

4049cost of kitchen cabinets</a>

4050 will vary depending on the type of wood and the varying degrees of <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/" target="_blank">

4051cabinet materials</a>

4052 used in the overall construction of the cabinet. Be prepared to pay at least $120 per square foot for wood kitchen cabinets.</p>

4053

4054

4055<p>

4056Stock kitchen cabinets that are readily available will be the most affordable, while semi-custom and custom cabinets will start to increase that base price depending on how personalized you want your cabinet set.</p>

4057

4058</div>

4059</div>

4060</div>

4061</div>

4096<div>

4097<p>

4098Whether the cabinets come pre-assembled or ready-to-assemble (RTA) will also impact the price as well as shipping costs, since pre-assembled wood cabinets will cost a lot more due to shipping weight.</p>

4099

4100

4101<p>

4102Vevano carries primarily engineered wood, which is less expensive than real hardwood, with many of the same benefits. A standard 10x10 kitchen cabinet set from Vevano Home starts at $2,000. The upper range for custom wood kitchen cabinets could get up to $7,000 - $10,000, if not more.</p>

4103

4104

4105<p>

4106Note that laminate cabinets are about half the cost of solid wood cabinets.</p>

4135Wood Cabinets: Pros &amp; Cons</h2>

4140</div>

4157✅ Pros</strong>

4158</span>

4159</p>

4160

4161

4162<ul>

4163

4164 <li>

4165Classic, beautiful appearance</li>

4166

4167 <li>

4168Sturdy, strong, and durable</li>

4169

4170 <li>

4171Variety of colors, grains, and <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-finishes/" target="_blank">

4172cabinet finishes</a>

4173</li>

4174

4175 <li>

4176available</li>

4177

4178 <li>

4179Every cabinet is unique since every piece of wood is unique</li>

4180

4181 <li>

4182Adds a natural, organic warmth to the room</li>

4183

4184 <li>

4185Long life-span</li>

4186

4187 <li>

4188Easy to find hardware to match</li>

4189

4190 <li>

4191Works well with most styles</li>

4193</ul>

4267<h2>

4268Cabinet Materials</h2>

4269

4270

4271<p>

4272While it&rsquo;s rare to have wood cabinets made entirely of solid wood, it&rsquo;s more common to have wood cabinets made with multiple materials.</p>

4273

4274</div>

4275</div>

4276</div>

4277</div>

4278<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-cc-baa-a-ab-abea">

4281<div>

4282<h3>

4283Solid Wood Cabinets</h3>

4284

4285</div>

4286</div>

4287</div>

4288</div>

4289<div class="">

4290<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-fcd-c-e-bdd-becbe">

4291<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-fcd-c-e-bdd-becbe">

4292<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4293<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4294<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-8__13d10 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4295<div class="">

4296<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-cbcfcb-ed-dda-b-afb">

4297<div class="merce-column-container">

4298<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-dac-ad--b-fedcd">

4299<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf dac-ad--b-fedcd-singleImageAlignment">

4300<img class="dac-ad--b-fedcd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/1AJnSKgAzXC_RVUkButtNJuV3CitqMgY_twbyjzbl_s/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci93b29kLWNhYmluZXQtdHlwZXMvc29saWQtd29vZC1jYWJpbmV0cy5qcGc" alt="cherry solid wood kitchen cabinets" title="cherry solid wood kitchen cabinets"/>

4301</div>

4302</div>

4303</div>

4304</div>

4305</div>

4306</div>

4307<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4308<div class="">

4309<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bd-ed-d--adaf">

4310<div>

4311</div>

4312</div>

4313</div>

4314</div>

4315</div>

4316</div>

4317</div>

4318</div>

4319</div>

4320<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-d-facf-b-bc-acbbf">

4321<div>

4322<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4323<div>

4324<p>

4325Solid wood cabinets featuring the singular natural material is the cream of the crop when it comes to wood cabinets. No two wood slabs are alike, featuring beautiful textures and wood grain. The range of colors available make wood a popular material for kitchen cabinets since it can work with so many styles. Real wood comes with the heftiest weight and the highest price tag since it&rsquo;s a premium material that&rsquo;s meant to last for decades.</p>

4326

4327

4328<p>

4329Solid wood is more likely to feature on the cabinet face frames and cabinet doors.</p>

4330

4356<div>

4357<h3>

4358Engineered Wood Cabinets</h3>

4359

4360</div>

4361</div>

4362</div>

4363</div>

4364<div class="">

4365<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ef-dca-dad-e-ddaad">

4366<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ef-dca-dad-e-ddaad">

4367<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4368<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4369<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-8__13d10 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4370<div class="">

4371<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-cc-e-a-e-efddc">

4372<div class="merce-column-container">

4373<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ecfdcb-db-e--cfc">

4374<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ecfdcb-db-e--cfc-singleImageAlignment">

4375<img class="ecfdcb-db-e--cfc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/ufBX__eVKmK4FnQEU-wkqNxOZEutc3bZXgY1qFQTVPA/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9Db2xsZWN0aW9ucy9DYWJpbmV0cy9XaWxvcmFQYWxvbWEvSW1hZ2UvQ29ydGluYUNvbmNoU2hlbGwyLmpwZw" alt="engineered wood cabinet doors" title="engineered wood cabinet doors"/>

4376</div>

4377</div>

4378</div>

4379</div>

4380</div>

4381</div>

4382<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4383<div class="">

4384<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-be-cb-f-aa-ca">

4385<div>

4386</div>

4387</div>

4388</div>

4389</div>

4390</div>

4391</div>

4392</div>

4393</div>

4394</div>

4395<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-caa-a-fa-b-bba">

4396<div>

4397<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4398<div>

4399<p>

4400Engineered wood can be found at almost any level of cabinet construction. Engineered wood is a man-made material that combines thinly sliced wood pieces into a slab fused together with heat and pressure, sometimes combined with melamine, to give it the appearance of wood.</p>

4401

4402

4403<p>

4404Despite not being pure wood, engineered wood is just as strong, lighter, less expensive, more waterproof, and more warp-resistant than solid wood. However, engineered wood cannot be refinished or painted.</p>

4405

4406</div>

4407</div>

4408</div>

4409</div>

4410</div>

4411</div>

4412</div>

4413</div>

4414</div>

4415</div>

4416</div>

4417</div>

4432<h3>

4433HDF &amp; MDF</h3>

4434

4435</div>

4436</div>

4437</div>

4438</div>

4439<div class="">

4440<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-dbe-e-f--ffdeed">

4441<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-dbe-e-f--ffdeed">

4442<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4443<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4444<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-8__13d10 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4445<div class="">

4446<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-eb-bfe---febdb">

4447<div class="merce-column-container">

4448<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-cdcbf-d--ac-dda">

4449<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf cdcbf-d--ac-dda-singleImageAlignment">

4450<img class="cdcbf-d--ac-dda-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/zNTOn_BeT2bX3CVvHu7-zABu0YseVBUBFLfs258R5SM/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9Db2xsZWN0aW9ucy9DYWJpbmV0cy9XaWxvcmFQYWxvbWEvSW1hZ2UvTWFycXVpc0dyYXlXb29kMS5qcGc" alt="painted grey cabinet doors" title="painted grey cabinet doors"/>

4451</div>

4452</div>

4453</div>

4454</div>

4455</div>

4456</div>

4457<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4458<div class="">

4459<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-dad--df-a-aeb">

4460<div>

4461</div>

4462</div>

4463</div>

4464</div>

4465</div>

4466</div>

4467</div>

4468</div>

4469</div>

4470<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ffdc-dd-f-a-bdcec">

4471<div>

4472<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4473<div>

4474<p>

4475High-density fiberboard (HDF) and medium-density fiberboard (MDF) are made by combining wood particles with resins and glue and pressing it together to create wood-like slabs in varying degrees of strength and density.</p>

4476

4477

4478<p>

4479High-density fiberboard (HDF) is one of the most common cabinet materials since it&rsquo;s strength parallels that of real wood. HDF is a common cabinet building material and can be found in cabinet panels.</p>

4480

4481

4482<p>

4483MDF is less dense than HDF and is mostly used for cabinet boxes, shelves, and drawer floors.</p>

4484

4485

4486<p>

4487Both HDF and MDF take paint well if you want to reface your cabinets, however, they lack the long lifespan of solid wood and engineered wood.</p>

4488

4516Plywood</h3>

4517

4518</div>

4533<img class="efa--fa-db-fffede-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/ENzpXNrubAruiy4oYeNCY7m-4WSSTe_aZx2MWUu_c48/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci93b29kLWNhYmluZXQtdHlwZXMvcGx5d29vZC1jYWJpbmV0cy5qcGc" alt="plywood cabinet doors" title="plywood cabinet doors"/>

4556<div>

4557<p>

4558<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/plywood-vs-particle-board/" target="_blank">

4559Plywood</a>

4560 is constructed of thin layers of wood, glued and pressed together. It&rsquo;s water resistant and can hold its weight without warping. Plywood also carries a cross-grain texture that&rsquo;s helpful to hold nails and screws.</p>

4561

4562

4563<p>

4564The inexpensive and lightweight plywood comes into play within cabinet and drawer boxes as inner box material. Plywood can also hold a veneer, giving the wood-look without the cost.</p>

In order to stain your kitchen cabinets, a high-quality hardwood base is needed and cannot be painted over.</p>

4899<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE--e-f--bbce">

4900<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf -e-f--bbce-singleImageAlignment">

4901<img class="-e-f--bbce-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/DUM5GTu21lQHntHy6_NSW4DEXHZG1mHlcySDGPD980c/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9Db2xsZWN0aW9ucy9DYWJpbmV0cy9XaWxvcmFIYXd0aG9ybmUvSW1hZ2UvU2hha2VyQ2luZGVyMS5qcGc" alt="veneered dark kitchen cabinets" title="veneered dark kitchen cabinets"/>

4902</div>

4903</div>

4904</div>

4905</div>

4906</div>

4907</div>

4908<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4909<div class="">

4910<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bddab-b-f-b-ddfec">

4911<div>

4912</div>

4913</div>

4914</div>

4915</div>

4916</div>

4917</div>

4918</div>

4919</div>

4920</div>

4921<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bca-f-da-a-ffaf">

4922<div>

4923<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4924<div>

4925<p>

4926A cabinet veneer, or a one-piece face, is constructed with a layer of real wood on top of a composite layer or plywood, reinforced with backing (paper, 2-3 ply wood, or resin) before application, giving it added strength and durability.</p>

4927

4928

4929<p>

4930Veneers can be made from a variety of wood species and various grades that affect how much it costs. A few assembly types are available that affect how the grain appears throughout your cabinets:</p>

4931

4932

4933<ul>

4934

4935 <li>

4936<strong>

4937<em>

4938Book match</em>

4939</strong>

4940 creates a mirrored grain appearance, like an open book.</li>

4941

4942 <li>

4943<em>

4944<strong>

4945Slip match</strong>

4946</em>

4947 lines up the cuts in the order they were sliced from the log.</li>

4948

4949 <li>

4950<em>

4951<strong>

4952Reverse slip match</strong>

4953</em>

4954 has every other leaf rotated 180 degrees.</li>

4955

4956 <li>

4957<em>

4958<strong>

4959Pleasing match</strong>

4960</em>

4961 are arranged by color consistency rather than grain matching.</li>

4962

4963 <li>

4964<em>

4965<strong>

4966Random match</strong>

4967</em>

4968 where undesired patterns are cut up and spread out.</li>

4969

4970</ul>

4971

4972

4973<p>

4974Often veneers are cut from a part of the tree that isn&rsquo;t easy to cut from or that have unique growth and knots, so the appearance can be truly one-of-a-kind and beautiful.</p>

4975

4976

4977<p>

4978Veneers are commonly found on cabinet doors and frames to maintain the classic appearance of a wood-look cabinet.</p>

4979

4980</div>

4981</div>

4982</div>

4983</div>

4984</div>

4985</div>

4986</div>

4987</div>

4988</div>

4989</div>

4990</div>

4991</div>

4992</div>

5006<h3>

5007Laminate Cabinets</h3>

5008

5009</div>

5010</div>

5011</div>

5012</div>

5013<div class="">

5014<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ec-cf-d-e-ceeedcc">

5015<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ec-cf-d-e-ceeedcc">

5016<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

5017<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

5018<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-8__13d10 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

5019<div class="">

5020<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bbbf--d-ae-ee">

5021<div class="merce-column-container">

5022<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-dd-cdf-a-bc-eec">

5023<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf dd-cdf-a-bc-eec-singleImageAlignment">

5024<img class="dd-cdf-a-bc-eec-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/zBtikQPKpRzY9Aj48H388swLbE301jYrfuMqitaN-Cg/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9Db2xsZWN0aW9ucy9DYWJpbmV0cy9XaWxvcmFQYWxvbWEvSW1hZ2UvTW9udGVDYXJsb0dsb3NzV2hpdGUyLmpwZw" alt="white laminate kitchen cabinets" title="white laminate kitchen cabinets"/>

5025</div>

5026</div>

5027</div>

5028</div>

5029</div>

5030</div>

5031<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-4__3eiub Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

5032<div class="">

5033<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-aefa-bc-e-ba-beef">

5034<div>

5035</div>

5036</div>

5037</div>

5038</div>

5039</div>

5040</div>

5041</div>

5042</div>

5043</div>

5044<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-eeaa-fa-f-a-faa">

5045<div>

5046<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

5047<div>

5048<p>

5049Laminate features a plastic layer on top of a composite layer that can be designed to look like real wood.</p>

5050

5051

5052<p>

5053Melamine is a laminate, or a substrate layer, sandwiched between paper fused with thermally fused melamine resin with high heat and pressure. Once it hardens, it creates a durable, scratch-resistant material that can be used to build sustainable and affordable cabinets that are easy to maintain.</p>

5054

5055

5056<p>

5057The paper fused to the substrate can feature printed colors, patterns, or wood designs to match the style you desire.</p>

5058
